for all the noobs making this by following the video (I say this because I was one of these noobs) 1) There is a written recipe for you to follow on Ro's website if you just look up "butterscotch cinnamon pie recipe" 2) She forgot to mention adding the buttermilk in the video but it's in the written recipe. I didn't do that and my dough was a completely dry flop as a result so ADD BUTTERMILK BEFORE CHILLING THE DOUGH AND AFTER MIXING THE BUTTER AND SHORTENING. I'm a complete baking newbie so maybe this goes without saying if you know what you're doing but just in case I help someone like me, I thought I'd say it anyway :)

Hello, I made this for Thanksgiving the other day. Here are some notes:  - The pie crust is very delicious. It'd be perfect in any other kind of pie. - The filling was overall... Kind of odd. It was very much a slightly more stabilized pudding texture and had a bit of a skin on the top (which tbh, I never minded on puddings.) The overall flavor was a bit lacking, to be honest. Every time I looked at it in the fridge, I wished it was a pumpkin pie, cause they look very similar. It's also quite difficult to cut out due to its texture, and due to the crust sticking to the bottom.   The takeaway is, use the pie crust in everything, and maybe use the filling for a pudding recipe

Instructions unclear : locked in an intergalactic prison for tampering with the barrier
Pie crust *in a mixing bowl -2.5 cups flour -2 tbsp sugar ---lightly mix -0.5 cups butter -0.5 cups shortening  -1 tbsp of water -1 tbsp vanilla extract ---use hands to FULLY mix (will take a while) *wrap in plastic wrap -chill two hours -flour your rolling pin and surface more than you think -roll out 0.25 inches thick and put into pan as she says (it may fall apart just fill in gaps) -push into sides of pan (you should be able to feel with your finger tips to make an even depth all around) -crimp edges or add the squares as she did -poke more holes than you think (all around sides too) -weight the pie with dried beans or rice, you can use wax paper too -bake at 350 for 35 minutes -remove pie weight -cook for another 15-20 minutes

Wow... This sucks.  Okay, so I followed the recipe as best as I could, and here is where I failed.  Crust, misread the butter labels, did not realize that one whole stick was half a cup so I used only half a stick.  Crust was too dry and crumbly to even become a crust.  Fail number two, forgot to add buttermilk early one.  Added buttermilk later, continued adding more buttermilk until the crust was at an consistency that it could actually be used.  The other half went much better, except that I forgot to add the sugar.  I nicked a piece of the pudding for a quick taste test after realizing this and felt that it tasted sweet enough.  I am much better with written instructions so I will be writing the instructions down from the video so I do not screw up attempt number two.  I will post again if my screw-up turns out to still taste good.

I made the pie according to what I saw in this video, and the filling never set. I left the pie to cool on my counter for an hour, then put it in my fridge for an hour, and then I put it in my FREEZER for another hour, and it was still liquid, it didn't even thicken to pancake-batter consistency.  I looked on your blog and the recipe is different there. Apparently I'm not supposed to take it off the heat as soon as I bring it to a boil, I'm suppose to leave it there boiling until it thickens on the stove. What is shortening?
I wrote down the whole recepie (except ingidients) in the metric temperature. Here it is: Crust:Put the Flour, salt, sugar, and vanilla in a bowl, then lightly mix it. Add butter, shortening, then kneed, it's okay for the dough to be dry. Wrap it up in plastic foil, then put in fridge for 2 hours. Then roll it out, so its half a centimeter thick. Roll the crust onto yoir rolling pin, then roll it out, off the rolling pin into the pie pan. Rip off the ecxess dough with your hands, and kneed down your dough into the pan so it is touching the edges everywhere. Take the ecxess dough, and roll it out. Then cut a very thick stripe out of it. Twist the stripe, and roll it lightly between your hands. Then put it around the edge of your crust, and kneed it in so it's stuck. If it doesn't go all the way around, make another. Poke holes with a fork in the bottom of the crust. Then take food wrap, the plastic kind thar doesnt melt and put inside your crust. Then fill it with non melting beans. Wrap the food wrap around itself, so it creates a block of beans inside your crust. This makes it hold its shape. Egg wash/brush on egg on the edge of the crust (1 yolk, 2 whites, pinch of salt). Then put it in the oven for 35 minutes at 175 degrees celcius. Then remove beans, and bake again for another 10-15 minutes. Then let the crust cool for a while. The filling sets quickly, so wait til you make it!!Filling:Mix egg yolks and corn starch, so it becomes a thick paste without lumps. Then add half the milk, mix it, then add the rest. Take everything except the crushed daim to the stove. Melt the butter over medium heat, add brown sugar cook for about 3 minutes. STIR CONSTANTLY! Then whisk in the cream, and add the yolk mixture you made earlier. Then salt and cinnamon. Keep on whisking, and bring it back off the stove. When the pot is still hot, add the crushed daim, and mix until it melts into the mixture. Then pour it into the crust.Finishing:Let the pie sit at room temperature for 1 hour, and then put it in the fridge for 2 hours. Now it's done! Serve with whipped cream.

try doing a cake based on the three routes(pacifist,neutral,genocide)and here is a layout i thought of:  top third(has crying asriel (pacifist),the exit door (neutral),or chara(genocide)) ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ middle third(has a puddle of tears(pacifist),crippled flowey(neutral) or dead flowey shreds(genocide)) ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ bottom third(has a dustless,crippled frisk holding a stick(pacifist),a not very dusty frisk holding a knife but not knowing what to do with it(neutral),or a really dusty frisk holding a dust and ketchup covered knife while wearing a locket and a red glow coming from their face(genocide))  ideas for the things:dust=fine sugar,ketchup=red icing,red glow=clear red icing(if you don't have that you can use thin streaks of normal icing) i spent so long on this and i am an undertale fan.this is just a nice idea.ingredients for decorations are covered.anything not mentioned is just what you'd normally use.like (or,in your case,rosanna pasino,love)if you think it will make a good video

For that pudding recipe I would suggest not to put yolk and cornstarch whisked together first since it did clump up and you can see it was at the bottom of the bowl. Instead mix the yolk with the milk and then whisk in cornstarch.  The cornstarch won't activate its thickening property unless it's cooked thoroughly (that's why it must come to a boil) and if it's left in clumps it will have a starchy taste in your mouth which is undesireable.
